EFTA00006591

---

This document page is a standard printed phone bill statement, likely generated by a phone service provider. It is a digital scan or photograph of a physical paper document, which is why it is not perfectly sharp or has blacked-out areas. However, the content and layout confirm it is a structured document page.

- It has a header with account and customer service information.
- A table lists call details (Date, Call Destination, Time, Number Called, Call Type, Minutes, Airtime Charges, Toll Charges, Total).
- Footnotes explain the call type abbreviations.
- A page number (Page 47 of 76) indicates it’s part of a larger document.
- The footer includes a document identifier (EFTA00006591).

The document is clearly structured to report on phone usage charges and does not contain any graphics, illustrations, or diagrams. Therefore, it is best classified as a document page. The entire text content is transcribed verbatim as requested, preserving all formatting and line breaks.

The document is from September 21, 2006, and covers calls on September 6, 2006. All charges are listed as $0, which may indicate a promotional plan or that the charges are not yet applied (e.g., pending or unposted).

Note: The "Number Called" column is completely blacked out in every row, which is common in privacy-protected documents. The transcription includes this as “[blacked out]” to preserve the original appearance.

- **Footnotes/Key**: Legend for “Call Type” provided at the bottom.
- **Document ID**: Footer text “EFTA00006595”, likely an internal reference number.

### Analysis of Content

- The table lists calls made on **September 7, 2006 (9/07/06)** and **September 8, 2006 (9/08/06)**.
- All charges are “$ -” (zero), indicating either the calls were free, or the charges were waived (possibly for Mobile2Mobile calls, which are often free within the same provider network — indicated by “(F)” in Call Type).

- The vast majority of calls were to “White Pls, NY” (White Plains, NY) or “Bronx Nyc, NY” (Bronx, New York City), which are local destinations within New York State, which aligns with “LOCAL AIRTIME” being the category.

## Analysis

This document is clearly a page from a phone bill or an itemized billing statement. Key indicators:

1.  **Structured Data**: It has a clear table format with headers (`Date`, `Call Destination`, `Time`, `Number Called`, `Call Type`, `Minutes`, `Airtme Charges`, `Toll Charges`, `Total`). The data entries are consistently aligned and formatted.
2.  **Contextual Text**: The title “LOCAL AIRTIME, LONG DISTANCE and INTERNATIONAL CHARGES - (Continued)” indicates this is a section of a larger bill. The footer “Call Type: (A) Call Waiting...” provides a legend for the call type codes.
3.  **Document Metadata**: Information such as “Customer Service Number”, “Oct 21, 2006”, and “Page 28 of 71” are typical of formal billing documents.
4.  **Typographical Consistency**: The text is printed with consistent fonts, line spacing, and alignment, which is characteristic of a printed page or a digital document exported from software, not a photograph of an illustration or a diagram.

**Therefore, this is a document page, not a photo or diagram.**

The transcription preserves all visible text, including line breaks and spacing as they appear in the original image.

EFTA00006642

---

This document is a page from an itemized phone bill, specifically page 42 of 71, showing charges for calls made on October 3, 2006. It includes columns for date, call destination, time, number called, call type, minutes, airtime charges, toll charges, and total charges. All charges in the table are listed as $ - (zero dollars).

The table contains 27 entries, most of which are calls to White Plains, NY, followed by calls to Bronx NYC, NY, and New York, NY. Many call types are marked with "(F)", which corresponds to "Mobile2Mobile" in the legend provided at the bottom. There are also a few "Incoming" entries.

The document includes a Customer Service Number and a date (Oct 21, 2006), which suggests this is the date the bill was generated or printed, not necessarily the date of the calls.

The top right corner indicates "Itemized Details For: Account Number:", but the account number is redacted.

There is also an alphanumeric identifier at the bottom right: EFTA00006642.

The document is structured as a table with clear headings and data entries. The layout, text formatting, and content are consistent with a printed or digital document generated by a telephone company for billing purposes.

## Decision

This is a document page. It is a structured, text-based itemized phone bill page, with clear headings, columns, and a table layout designed for readability and record-keeping. It is not a photo or diagram, but a formal document with a specific purpose: to itemize charges for phone usage.

## Document Type Analysis

This appears to be a **document page** — specifically, a page from a printed or digitally generated phone bill statement.

**Reasoning**:
- The layout is tabular and highly structured with columns and rows.
- It contains headers, footnotes, and sequential data entries.
- There are clear page numbers (“Page 53 of 71”) and a customer service number.
- The content includes structured data (date, time, destination, call type, minutes, charges), characteristic of an itemized bill.
- The text is legible and formatted in a consistent way, typical of printed or digital billing documents.

The page includes:
- Header information: Customer Service Number, date, page number.
- Title: “LOCAL AIRTIME, LONG DISTANCE and INTERNATIONAL CHARGES - (Continued)”.
